<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Format">Format</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/dota2/index.php?title=ESL/UK_Premiership/2020/Autumn&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Format">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li><b>Participants</b>
<ul><li>Teams must have a minimum of three players residing in <span class="flag"><a href="/dota2/Category:United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom"><img alt="United Kingdom" src="/commons/images/5/5e/Gb_hd.png" width="36" height="24" loading="lazy" /></a></span> <a target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener" class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Great_Britain">Great Britain</a> or <span class="flag"><a href="/dota2/Category:Ireland" title="Ireland"><img alt="Ireland" src="/commons/images/2/2c/Ie_hd.png" width="36" height="24" loading="lazy" /></a></span> <a target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener" class="external text" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ireland">Ireland</a></li></ul></li>
<li><b>Group Stage</b>
<ul><li>Single round-robin</li>
<li>All matches are <abbr title="Best-of-two">Bo2</abbr></li>
<li><span style="background-color:rgb(221,244,221);">1st and 2nd place teams</span> proceed to the Playoff Semifinal</li>
<li><span style="background-color:rgb(249,240,199);">3rd to 6th place teams </span> proceed to the Playoff Quarterfinals</li>
<li><span style="background-color:rgb(251,223,223);">Bottom two teams</span> are eliminated</li></ul></li>
<li><b>Playoffs</b>
<ul><li>Single-elimination bracket</li>
<li>Grand Final is <abbr title="Best-of-five">Bo5</abbr>, all other matches are <abbr title="Best-of-three">Bo3</abbr></li></ul></li></ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Broadcast_Talent">Broadcast Talent</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/dota2/index.php?title=ESL/UK_Premiership/2020/Autumn&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Broadcast Talent">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<ul><li><b>Commentators:</b>
<ul><li><span class="flag"><a href="/dota2/Category:United_States" title="United States"><img alt="United States" src="/commons/images/3/3b/Us_hd.png" width="36" height="24" loading="lazy" /></a></span>&#160;<a href="/dota2/Bkop" title="Bkop">Bkop</a>&#160;(Benjamin Kopilow)</li>
<li><span class="flag"><a href="/dota2/Category:United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom"><img alt="United Kingdom" src="/commons/images/5/5e/Gb_hd.png" width="36" height="24" loading="lazy" /></a></span>&#160;<a href="/dota2/MoFarah" title="MoFarah">MoFarah</a>&#160;(Jack Williams)</li>
<li><span class="flag"><a href="/dota2/Category:United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom"><img alt="United Kingdom" src="/commons/images/5/5e/Gb_hd.png" width="36" height="24" loading="lazy" /></a></span>&#160;<a href="/dota2/Nomad" title="Nomad">Nomad</a>&#160;(Jared Bajina)</li>
<li><span class="flag"><a href="/dota2/Category:United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom"><img alt="United Kingdom" src="/commons/images/5/5e/Gb_hd.png" width="36" height="24" loading="lazy" /></a></span>&#160;<a href="/dota2/TeaGuvnor" title="TeaGuvnor">TeaGuvnor</a>&#160;(Robson Merritt)</li>
<li><span class="flag"><a href="/dota2/Category:United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom"><img alt="United Kingdom" src="/commons/images/5/5e/Gb_hd.png" width="36" height="24" loading="lazy" /></a></span>&#160;<a href="/dota2/index.php?title=Crysen&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Crysen (page does not exist)">Crysen</a>&#160;(Jon Bennett)</li></ul></li></ul>
